4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes Ingress v1beta1 to v1 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement Ingress API handling for both v1beta1 and v1: the conversion functions between versions, the validation changes (pathType became required), and the storage version migration logic.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

## Findings

### Conversion Functions (v1beta1 ↔ v1)

**networking/v1beta1 path:**
- `pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/conversion.go` — hand-written conversions handling `ServiceName`/`ServicePort` → `Service.Name`/`Service.Port` structural difference
- `pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go` — auto-generated top-level `Convert_v1beta1_Ingress_To_networking_Ingress` etc.

**networking/v1 path:**
- `pkg/apis/networking/v1/zz_generated.conversion.go` — auto-generated `Convert_v1_Ingress_To_networking_Ingress`, `Convert_networking_Ingress_To_v1_Ingress` etc.

**extensions/v1beta1 (legacy) path:**
- `pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/conversion.go` + `zz_generated.conversion.go`

### Validation Changes (pathType became required)

- `pkg/apis/networking/validation/validation.go` — `ValidateIngressSpec` requires non-nil `pathType`; `IngressValidationOptions` handles beta→GA update leniency
- `pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/defaults.go` — `SetDefaults_HTTPIngressPath` defaults `pathType` to `ImplementationSpecific` in v1beta1

### Storage Version Migration

- `pkg/apis/networking/install/install.go` — sets `v1` as highest priority version via `SetVersionPriority`
- `pkg/registry/networking/ingress/strategy.go` — covers all three API versions in `GetResetFields`, calls validation
- `pkg/registry/networking/ingress/storage/storage.go` — REST storage wiring

Key functions: `Convert_v1beta1_IngressBackend_To_networking_IngressBackend`, `Convert_networking_IngressBackend_To_v1beta1_IngressBackend`, `Convert_v1beta1_IngressSpec_To_networking_IngressSpec`, `Convert_networking_IngressSpec_To_v1beta1_IngressSpec`.\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go**: Auto-generated functions including `Convert_v1beta1_Ingress_To_networking_Ingress`, `Convert_networking_Ingress_To_v1beta1_Ingress`, and `RegisterConversions`.\\n\\n### networking/v1 <-> internal networking\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/v1/zz_generated.conversion.go**: Auto-generated `Convert_v1_Ingress_To_networking_Ingress`, `Convert_networking_Ingress_To_v1_Ingress`, `Convert_v1_IngressSpec_To_networking_IngressSpec`, `Convert_networking_IngressSpec_To_v1_IngressSpec`.\\n\\n### extensions/v1beta1 <-> internal networking (legacy path)\\n- **pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/conversion.go**: Hand-written conversions mirroring the networking/v1beta1 ones for the older extensions API group.\\n- **pkg/apis/extensions/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go**: Auto-generated `Convert_v1beta1_Ingress_To_networking_Ingress`, `Convert_networking_Ingress_To_v1beta1_Ingress`.\\n\\n## 2. Validation Changes (pathType became required in v1)\\n\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/validation/validation.go**: The key change is in `ValidateIngressSpec` \u2014 `pathType` is required (returns `field.Required` error when nil). The `IngressValidationOptions` struct controls beta-to-GA transitions: `AllowInvalidSecretName` and `AllowInvalidWildcardHostRule`. `ValidateIngressCreate` uses strict options; `ValidateIngressUpdate` uses helper functions to permit previously-stored invalid values during updates.\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/v1beta1/defaults.go**: `SetDefaults_HTTPIngressPath` defaults `pathType` to `ImplementationSpecific` for v1beta1 objects, bridging the semantic gap to the required field in v1.\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/validation/validation_test.go**: Comprehensive tests for validation, including pathType scenarios.\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/fuzzer/fuzzer.go**: Ensures `HTTPIngressPath.PathType` is always non-nil during fuzzing (required for round-trip conversion tests).\\n\\n## 3. Storage Version Migration Logic\\n\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/install/install.go**: Sets version priority with `scheme.SetVersionPriority(v1, v1beta1, v1alpha1)`, making networking.k8s.io/v1 the preferred/storage version.\\n- **pkg/registry/networking/ingress/storage/storage.go**: The REST storage implementation wiring together strategy, using the internal networking type for storage (converted to/from v1 as the storage version).\\n- **pkg/registry/networking/ingress/strategy.go**: `ingressStrategy` implements `GetResetFields` covering all three API versions (`extensions/v1beta1`, `networking.k8s.io/v1beta1`, `networking.k8s.io/v1`), calls `ValidateIngressCreate`/`ValidateIngressUpdate`, and manages spec/status field separation.\\n\\n## Supporting Files\\n\\n- **pkg/apis/networking/types.go**: Internal type definitions (`PathType`, `Ingress`, `IngressSpec`, `IngressBackend`, `IngressServiceBackend`).\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/networking/v1/types.go**: Published v1 API types where `pathType` is required.\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/networking/v1beta1/types.go**: Published v1beta1 API types where `pathType` is optional (defaults to ImplementationSpecific).\"\n}\n",
